***maken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a> (141)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:macon.html>macon</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*mak≈çn</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fix, to repair, to mend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take (a photo)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mackelijc</i>, a <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> Hollandic form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gemackelijc</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemak.html>gemak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">ease</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:makken.html>makken</a> (40537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:makken.html>makken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bargoens" class="extiw" title="w:Bargoens">Bargoens</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend money
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>Wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:allure.html>allure</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:welgesteld.html>welgesteld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezin.html>gezin</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigenlijk.html>eigenlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> cent <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:makken.html>makken</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:airs.html>airs</a> of a well-to-do family, but actually <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> not have a cent to <b>spend</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Only found in the expressions <i><a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:makken.html>makken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> ("have nothing to spend") or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> cent <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:makken.html>makken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> ("have not [<a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a>] a cent to spend").</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:makker.html>makker</a> (2127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">macker</i>, probably from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*gemacke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">companion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">make</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">match</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:makker.html>makker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:makkers.html>makkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:makkertje.html>makkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:mate.html>mate</a>, fellow, colleague, companion, (not very close) friend, ally etc.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***makreel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:makreel.html>makreel</a> (38048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">makereel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">maquerel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:makreel.html>makreel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:makrelen.html>makrelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:makreeltje.html>makreeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>mackerel, <i>Scomber scombrus</i></li>
<li>Any fish of the family Scombridae.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>mal</a> (5452)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_13">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>mal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mallen.html>mallen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>malletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>mold, cast <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">device to help creating shapes</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>mal</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>maller</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">malst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>foolish, crazy, lacking common sense</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The adjective <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>mal</a></i> always refers to an aspect of a thing or person. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the adjective form of the noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mallerd.html>mallerd</a></i>. For other senses, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dom</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gek.html>gek</a></i> are used.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:malaise.html>malaise</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:malaise.html>malaise</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="id"><a href = vnd.unilang:malaise.html>malaise</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Latn headword" lang="id">malais√™</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">economics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">depression</span>, a period of major economic contraction.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:malaise.html>malaise</a></span>, a feeling of general bodily discomfort, fatigue or unpleasantness, often at the onset of illness.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">malarde</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mawdelare</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">malart</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mallart</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">wild duck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly derived from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">Madelhart</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">proper name</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">whence the English forms <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">maudelard</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mawdelard</i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>; or alternatively from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">male</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:malle.html>malle</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">male</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ard</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mallard.html>mallard</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mallards</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:mallard.html>mallard</a></strong></b>)

<p>From obsolete <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">–º–∞–º–∞–Ω—Ç</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mamant</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">–º–∞–º–æ–Ω—Ç</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mamont</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), probably from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uralic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Uralic languages">Uralic</a></span> language.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***man.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> (102)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mann-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_12">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mans.html>mans</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mannetje.html>mannetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:manneke.html>manneke</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">manneken</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></a>, human male, either adult or age-irrespective
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oude.html>oude</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zee.html>zee</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:The_Old_Man_and_the_Sea" class="extiw" title="w:en:The Old Man and the Sea">The Old <b><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a></b> and the Sea</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>husband, male spouse</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The normal plural <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a></i>. The unchanged form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used after numerals only; it refers to the size of a group rather than a number of individuals. For example: <i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:totaal.html>totaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verloren.html>verloren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> 5000 <u><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></u> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a>.</i> (‚Äú5000 <u><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a></u> altogether <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> their <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a> in that battle.‚Äù) The plural <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mans.html>mans</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> dated, now mostly occurring in nautical contexts or in dialect.</li>
<li>Compound <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> with <i>-man</i> as their last component often take <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lieden.html>lieden</a></i> or <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lui.html>lui</a></i> in the plural, rather than <i>-mannen</i>. For example: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandweerman.html>brandweerman</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">firefighter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> ‚Üí <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandweerlieden.html>brandweerlieden</a></i> (alongside <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandweerlui.html>brandweerlui</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandweermannen.html>brandweermannen</a></i>).</li>
<li>Various alternative diminutives exist, including <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:manneke.html>manneke</a></i> (used especially in Flanders) and the dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mannechie</i>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijn.html>mandarijn</a> (27553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">mandarim</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms">menteri</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms">manteri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">‡§Æ‡§®‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mantri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">‡§Æ‡§®‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§®‡•ç</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mantrin</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">minister, councillor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijn.html>mandarijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijnen.html>mandarijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijntje.html>mandarijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A mandarin, Far Eastern (notably Chinese Imperial) high official</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pundit, someone in/with authority
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijnen.html>mandarijnen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:schaden.html>schaadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reputatie.html>reputatie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brui.html>brui</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>moest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>geven</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>pundits</b> ruined his reputation so badly he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> to call it quits.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***mandrake.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mandrake.html>mandrake</a> (27048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mandragora</i>, with <i>-dragora</i> reinterpreted as related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dragon</i> and replaced with native <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:drake.html>drake</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandrake.html>mandrake</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mandrakes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mandragora, a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of tiny <a href = vnd.unilang:demon.html>demon</a> immune to fire.</li>
<li>Any plant of the genus <i>Mandragora</i>, certain of which are <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> to have medicinal properties; the root of these plants often resembles the shape of a small person, hence occasioning various mythic, magical, or occult uses.</li>
<li>A root of a <a href = vnd.unilang:mandrake.html>mandrake</a> plant that resembled human form, especially one kept or used for magic or occult purposes.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1936</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:rollo.html>Rollo</a> Ahmed,  <cite>The Black Art</cite>, London |  Long, page 75:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b>Mandrakes</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> sometimes considered in the light of familiars. Witches kept both male and female <a href = vnd.unilang:specimens.html>specimens</a> of the magic root in bottles[.]</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The drug methaqualone.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">mandies</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plural</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<div class="NavFrame">
<div class="NavHead" style="text-align: left;">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></div>
<div class="NavContent derivedterms" style="text-align: left; column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">American <a href = vnd.unilang:mandrake.html>mandrake</a></span></li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">maniaque</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">maniacus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ŒºŒ±ŒΩŒπŒ±Œ∫œåœÇ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maniak√≥s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, adjectival form of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ŒºŒ±ŒΩŒØŒ±</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">man√≠a</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">madness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***mank.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mank.html>mank</a> (12536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">manc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">a limping or lame person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mancus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">maimed or defective</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*man-ko-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">maimed in the hand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*man-</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mank.html>mank</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mank.html>manker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">mankst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lame</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:mank.html>mank</a></b>
